    function Post(obj) {
      var name = obj.name;
      if (obj.checked) {
          val = obj.value;
      } else {
          val = "";
      }
      // hidden追加
      $('<input>').attr({
          'type': 'hidden',
          'name': name,
          'value': val
      }).appendTo($('#frmSearch'));
      $('#frmSearch').submit();
    }

                                <div class="getInfo"><h3>Card Set(s)</h3>-ADVENTURE ON KAMI&#039;S ISLAND- [OP15-EB04]</div>                
                <a href="javascript:void(0);" class="commonBtn cardViewBtn"><span>CARD VIEW</span></a>
              </div>
            </dd>
          </dl>
